# Phase 6 restaurant decisions

Primary-orchestrator scoring began 2026-07-17 after the Phase 5 gate passed. Every numeric rubric value below is an **orchestrator estimate** grounded in the cited accepted evidence; literal ratings and prices remain source-documented metadata. Missing or process-sparse evidence is routed to `score-unresolved`, never converted into a low score. Positive disqualifications cite the accepted adverse fact. The user-authorized U.S. preference screen is recorded separately as `US-standardized-chain-low-novelty`; fast service, low price, and multi-location status alone never trigger it.

Score tuple: `P/V/Src/C/O = S_scratch`; interestingness tuple: `δ/scarcity/technique/review-novelty/polarization = I`. `G = √(S×I)` is computed only after both axes are supported. Rating-unconfirmed scratch venues remain surfaced in their explicit tier.

## Primary decision — Phase 5 evidence-exhausted universe

Primary decision for every row below: **evidence-exhausted-no-score**. The required evidence sequence was completed, but current identity or score-bearing evidence remains unavailable. No missing field is converted into a zero, disqualification, low-novelty finding, or negative production inference. Each record remains terminal for this run and is excluded from numeric ranking while preserving its individual reason and source.

## Phase 6 completion audit — 2026-07-17

- Population reconciliation: **1,644 Phase 5 IDs = 1,644 decision IDs**, all unique; missing 0, unexpected 0, duplicates 0.
- Terminal dispositions: **225 scoreable**, **1,107 score-unresolved**, **219 evidence-exhausted-no-score**, **55 reversible user-preference exclusions**, **33 positive DQs**, and **5 canonical duplicates**.
- Evidence linkage: every decision ID exists exactly once in `05-evidence-ledger.md`; each batch declares that ledger/raw-evidence row as its evidence basis, and individually exceptional/DQ/duplicate rows preserve their scoped rationale.
- Arithmetic: every scoreable row has S, I and G; all `G = sqrt(S×I)` values match to one decimal; every explicit five-part vector sums to its printed total and respects the criterion maxima. The two calibration anchors below S60 are explicitly marked `not ranked`; no other scoreable row is below S60.
- Positive-DQ gate: all 33 remaining DQs contain affirmative closure, explicit no-food/snack-only scope, outside-vendor/off-site production, uncooked-retail, or equivalent positive evidence. Seven absence-based DQs were corrected to unresolved during this audit.
- Missing-evidence gate: all 1,107 process/rating/status-sparse accepted records and all 219 evidence-exhausted records remain unscored; none received a low numeric score or DQ merely because evidence was absent.
- Preference gate: all 55 exclusions are explicitly reversible, separate from DQ, and cite positive standardized/familiar U.S. format evidence; fast service, low price and multi-location status alone were not used.
- Duplicate gate: R-0877→R-1179, R-1232→R-1128, R-1464→R-1323, R-2298→R-2773 and R-2923→R-1493 each point to an extant canonical decision and are ranked once.
- Product/service boundary: beverage production, entertainment cadence, counter service, delivery/takeaway format and isolated product evidence were not silently promoted into restaurant production or used alone as negative verdicts.

**Phase 6 gate: PASS.**
